OVERVIEW: Tests framework clang modules in a clean environment.

USAGE: modules-verifier <framework> [--sdk <sdk>] [--clang <clang>] [--target <target> ...] [--target-variant <target-variant> ...] [--language <language> ...] [--standard <standard> ...] [--diagnostic-filename-map <diagnostic-filename-map>] [--intermediates-directory <intermediates-directory>] [--verbose] [--enable-local-submodule-visibility] -- [<additional-clang-arguments> ...]

ARGUMENTS:
<framework>             The framework to be tested.
<additional-clang-arguments>
Additional arguments to pass to clang.

OPTIONS:
--sdk <sdk>             Path to the SDK. If not provided, the SDKROOT
environment variable (set by `xcrun`) will be used.
--clang <clang>         Path to clang, defaults to the one specified by the
SDK.
--target <target>       Target to pass to clang, e.g. x86_64-apple-macos13.0,
arm64-apple-ios16.0, arm64-apple-ios16.0-macabi, etc.
Can be specified multiple times.
--target-variant <target-variant>
Target variant to pass to clang, e.g.
x86_64-apple-ios16.0-macabi. Can be specified
multiple times.
--language <language>   Language to test, can be specified multiple times.
Values are ["c", "c++", "objective-c",
"objective-c++"]. (values: c, c++, objective-c,
objective-c++; default: objective-c)
--standard <standard>   Language standard/dialect to test, can be specified
multiple times. Values are ["ansi", "c89", "gnu89",
"c99", "gnu99", "c11", "gnu11", "c17", "gnu17",
"c++98", "gnu++98", "c++11", "gnu++11", "c++14",
"gnu++14", "c++17", "gnu++17", "c++20", "gnu++20",
"c++23", "gnu++23", "c++26", "gnu++26"]. (values:
ansi, c89, gnu89, c99, gnu99, c11, gnu11, c17, gnu17,
c++98, gnu++98, c++11, gnu++11, c++14, gnu++14,
c++17, gnu++17, c++20, gnu++20, c++23, gnu++23,
c++26, gnu++26; default: gnu17, gnu++20)
--diagnostic-filename-map <diagnostic-filename-map>
JSON file to map file paths in diagnostics, e.g. from
paths in $(BUILT_PRODUCTS_DIR) to $(SRCROOT). Exact
format is internal to Xcode and subject to change.
--intermediates-directory <intermediates-directory>
Directory for intermediate testing files, logs, etc.
--verbose               Emit extra diagnostics, such as ones produced by
dependencies.
--enable-local-submodule-visibility
Experimental - has known compatibility issues with
Objective-C frameworks in clang 14.0.x. Runs an
additional test using local submodule visibility (a
stricter mode with include-what-you-use semantics).
--version               Show the version.
-h, --help              Show help information.
